  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_796da908-022f-4009-b66b-8b0ada0f54cb'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer5653359347538872689">He is an ancient vampire, bound by a savage curse. <br/>She is a twenty-nine-year-old agent of homeland security, investigating a dangerous cult. <br/>Theirs is a Blood Destiny about to unfold... <br/><br/>Descended from the progeny of Celestial Gods and humans, Nathaniel Silivasi is handsome, seductive, and powerful beyond measure: a lethal vampire.   <span id="freeText5653359347538872689" style="display:none">He is an ancient vampire, bound by a savage curse. <br />She is a twenty-nine-year-old agent of homeland security, investigating a dangerous cult. <br />Theirs is a Blood Destiny about to unfold... <br /><br />Descended from the progeny of Celestial Gods and humans, Nathaniel Silivasi is handsome, seductive, and powerful beyond measure: a lethal vampire. Belonging to an ancient civilization that sacrificed its females to the verge of extinction, he is also cursed. Like all the sons of Jadon, he is incapable of producing female offspring and required to sacrifice a first born son as atonement for the sins of his forefathers. While he belongs to a modern civilization, he is bound by primeval law. <br /><br />When Jocelyn Levi stumbles upon Nathaniel's pristine mountain valley, she is not prepared for the collision of worlds she is about to encounter. As an agent of the homeland security department, ICE, the beautiful, defiant female has an agenda of her own: to stop the ritualistic slaughter of innocent young women by a human trafficking ring. Little does she know, the evil she seeks is unlike anything she has ever witnessed. She has entered a world of warriors, code, and mystery, where the predators are divided only by degrees of light and shadow, and the dark handsome stranger who has come to her aid is the most dangerous of all.</span>

<div id="review_675983129" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/675983129" />
    <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake"><img alt="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605987751p2/11626803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/675983129?book_show_action=true">Jul 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake">Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=captivity">captivity</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer675983129" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9482602201017949663"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/>So like I said in one of my status updates on this thing, it was...well, it was bloody. <br/><br/>Like we might as well be in the stands of an Alabama football game what with the flood of crimson that leaked from these pages. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467159860i/19559461._SY540_.jpg' width='421' height='545' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>For serious though, I feel like just even talking about it requires a disclaimer. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467159860i/19559462._SX540_.jpg' width='423' height='317.25' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>We had detailed torture, murder, and mayhem...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467159860ra/19559464.gif' width='500' height='211' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Some really awful shit happening to some innocent people...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467159860ra/19559463.gif' width='500' height='268' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>And to some not so innocent people too. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467161337ra/19559576.gif' width='500' height='267' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>*<br/>*<br/>*<br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459695690ra/18644040.gif' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I know, right?<br/><br/><br/>...Luckily, I have no problem </span>
  <span id="freeText9482602201017949663" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br><br>So like I said in one of my status updates on this thing, it was...well, it was bloody. <br><br>Like we might as well be in the stands of an Alabama football game what with the flood of crimson that leaked from these pages. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467159860i/19559461._SY540_.jpg" width="421" height="545" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For serious though, I feel like just even talking about it requires a disclaimer. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467159860i/19559462._SX540_.jpg" width="423" height="317.25" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We had detailed torture, murder, and mayhem...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467159860ra/19559464.gif" width="500" height="211" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Some really awful shit happening to some innocent people...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467159860ra/19559463.gif" width="500" height="268" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>And to some not so innocent people too. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467161337ra/19559576.gif" width="500" height="267" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*<br>*<br>*<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1459695690ra/18644040.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I know, right?<br><br><br>...Luckily, I have no problem with this...as I am heartless with no soul. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452626113ra/17719425.gif" width="500" height="210" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>However, if you <i>do</i> have an...aversion to somewhat descriptive bloody scenes, I would avoid this one if I were you. <br><br>So there's that. <br><br>Otherwise, I thought this was a pretty interesting twist on the "same old" Vampire story. <br><br>I have been reading Vampire books since the early 1990's...<br><br>WAAAAAY before a certain "sparkly" vampire decided to attend Forks High and get pussy whipped. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467161337ra/19559577.gif" width="400" height="227" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That's right. <br><br>Believe it or not, Twi-hards, this was a romance genre looooooong before Miss Meyer arrived on the scene. <br><br>And I'm not just talking about Anne Rice and Bon Temps either. <br><br>I'm talking about the <i>Dark Series</i> by Christine Feehan, <i>The Last Vampire</i> Series by Christopher Pike, and countless others. <br><br>Anyway, my point is that I have been reading Vampire/PNR romance for a loooooong time. #NerdAlert<br><br>And they <i>all</i> usually have their own "twist" on the whole thing. <br><br>How they came to be.<br>How they live in the human world. <br>Are they secret? <br>Living in the open?<br>Sometimes sunlight hurts them, sometimes not.<br>Sometimes they can turn anyone, other times people have to be "compatible..."<br>Sometimes they can heal with their blood, the fucking dirt of the Carpathian Mountains, or just their own damned saliva. <br><br>I think I've read so many different variations, it's ridiculous. <br><br>And I don't really fucking care. <br> <br>Because...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467161337ra/19559578.gif" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Needless to say, the fact that Tessa Dawn was able to come up with a whole new twist on this <i>ish</i> that I thought was pretty interesting was....well, pretty interesting. <br><br>I wasn't so sure how that whole "first son" thing would pan out, but it seemed to go aight. <br><br>Also, I didn't love the heroine...and the story did seem to get bogged down by that first-book-in-the-series parry of confusion followed by the proverbial thrust of information overload. <br><br>But I always give first series books a pass on that as there is a lot of world building to be done and all that jazz. <br><br>Other than that, I thought this was a very interesting, well written read and I am really interested in Marquis' story, which I believe is next...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467162115ra/19559601.gif" width="245" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Find me at:<br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/SteamyReadsBlog/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473872687i/20525702.jpg" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow us on facebook" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.instagram.com/steamyreads/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473872687i/20525703.jpg" width="40" height="40" alt="Follow us on instagram" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shelly Strange" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shelly Strange" href="/user/show/25393430-shelly-strange">Shelly Strange</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Shelly Strange by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1649446192" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6330532210336115765"><b>Okay. Brrrrt. Back it up.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467740580ra/19625199.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>What caused me to rage DNF this ended up being one of those instances where the thing that happened was not what it appeared to be. (Thanks for enlightening me, Casey.) So I was able to finish the book. I'll leave the spoiler because the scene was still disturbing and rage-inducing, but I was so glad to know there was more going on there. <br/><br/>This is the scene that happens around 56%.<br/><br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[THEN, the one interesting vampire character that I thought was funny and sexy</span></span>
  <span id="freeText6330532210336115765" style="display:none"><b>Okay. Brrrrt. Back it up.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467740580ra/19625199.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What caused me to rage DNF this ended up being one of those instances where the thing that happened was not what it appeared to be. (Thanks for enlightening me, Casey.) So I was able to finish the book. I'll leave the spoiler because the scene was still disturbing and rage-inducing, but I was so glad to know there was more going on there. <br><br>This is the scene that happens around 56%.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[THEN, the one interesting vampire character that I thought was funny and sexy basically rapes a young human woman who is madly in love with him. She tells him she loves him. He rejects her at first, then propositions her for a sex-only thing, she says yes because she will take anything he will give her, then gets scared in the middle of it because she is still a virgin. She tries to tell him no, tries to push him away, actually does end up telling him flat out "I'm a virgin" and then that turns him on even more and he impales himself in her while she is totally dry and not aroused. And then leaves right after he gets off inside her, leaving her a bloody and semen-coated mess. FUCK YOU ASSHOLE!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!<br><br><i>That ended up being the evil bad guy who took the appearance of the non-evil vampire. </i>  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I still hated Jocelyn, though. She was one of the worst female heroines I've ever read in a PNR. *eyeroll* <br><br>She's shown miracles, she gets this <b>
  <i>birthmark of a constellation</i>
</b> on her arm spontaneously, the moon changes colors, a constellation appears in the sky, she witnesses a brutal murder and supernatural birth of a demon child, finds out vampires are real, sees them do things no human can do, yet she can't think <i>maybe Nathaniel is telling her the truth?</i> Not even to just CONSIDER IT??? A little?? Nerp. <br><br>Then she goes off with the OBVIOUS bad guy like an IDIOT. And then realizes right away, <i>Der der, uh-oh, I was safer where I was</i>. YEAH, YOU THINK. It was pretty obvious. So unbelievable. She sees with her OWN EYES what the evil vampires do to women like her (the special snowflake ones) and she finds good ones who will protect her, gets further VERIFICATION of that from one of their wives, and then OF COURSE she still runs from them. <br><br>And then she still does more stupid stuff. I just could not stand her. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467532260ra/19601973.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>But I'm actually glad I finished it. I liked the other vampires. There is potential. My favorite is Marquis, but I also liked Nachari. I like how the vampires can control the elements. They are much more powerful than any vampires I've ever read about. <br><br>The romance was the worst part of it. Too cheesy for my tastes. But the blood and gore was fun. Decapitation? Pffft. Too tame for these guys. Merely staking through the heart? Pffft. Child's play. <br><br>So I will probably try book two after all. The Blood Curse is kind of cheesy, but I think I can get over it. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Male vamp meets his mate and within 30 days must turn her and she magically conceives twins and gives birth to them in 48 hours. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467398329i/19588706.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Original post:<br><br>Buddy read with the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148935-dust-off-your-machalo-it-s-time-for-another-buddy-read" rel="nofollow noopener">MacHalo</a> group. And also because Jilly and Val, and it seems like lots of people have been reading this lately. I love vampires. I hope I like it. *fingers crossed*<br><br><b>Vampire month begins! Don't be sucky, books!</b></b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/665071770" />
    <a title="Kristen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen"><img alt="Kristen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1312922334p2/5477946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/665071770?book_show_action=true">Jul 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristen" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen">Kristen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/10067360-blood-destiny">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Kristen by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/5808260-carrie-badass-alpha-male-cowboy-connoisseur">Carrie (Badass, Alpha-male, Cowboy Connoisseur )</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=fated-to-be-mated">fated-to-be-mated</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=great-ending">great-ending</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=dark-hero">dark-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=family-dynamic">family-dynamic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=humorous">humorous</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=couldnt-put-down">couldnt-put-down</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer665071770" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4142111921201561736"><b>4 to 4 1/2 THRILLING stars</b><br/><br/>OMG!!! I'm at a loss for words to describe my feeling about this book. <i>Blood Destiny</i> is one of the most intense, shocking, and thrilling stories I've read. I was intrigued, I was captivated, and I was repulsed, not to mention grossed out by the animalistic violence in this dark paranormal romance. <br/><br/><b><i>Blood Destiny</i> is more horror than romance though, which the horror-movie-junkie in me loved.</b> It's brutal and gruesome in its explicit mayhem (just think of the movie Saw) and </span>
  <span id="freeText4142111921201561736" style="display:none"><b>4 to 4 1/2 THRILLING stars</b><br /><br />OMG!!! I'm at a loss for words to describe my feeling about this book. <i>Blood Destiny</i> is one of the most intense, shocking, and thrilling stories I've read. I was intrigued, I was captivated, and I was repulsed, not to mention grossed out by the animalistic violence in this dark paranormal romance. <br /><br /><b><i>Blood Destiny</i> is more horror than romance though, which the horror-movie-junkie in me loved.</b> It's brutal and gruesome in its explicit mayhem (just think of the movie Saw) and graphic ritual scenes. The vampires in this story, even the good ones, are very true to their nature. There is no paranormal fluff in this book. With that said, the author countered the book's intensity with brilliant humor (I loved Braden) and also some romance and steam toward the end. <br /><br /><i>Blood Destiny</i> is an extremely well written, character driven, action packed dark paranormal romance. <b>I loved this book but it is <u>NOT FOR THE FAINT OF HEART!</u> I can not stress that enough!!!</b> If you're looking for a darker, edgier read <u>with a splash of romance</u>, you might want to consider giving this book a try. I also suggest reading other reviews to get a good sense of what awaits you. <br /><br /><b>Caution: There is a rape scene I found troubling (not heroine). Please use discretion before reading this book.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="4142111921201561736" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13869613078988126516"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464216650i/19213611.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Rape, Torture, Murder, Dismemberment, Bloody Battles, and Explicit Sex... This book has it all!<br/><br/>If you like Paranormal Romance, but also want to bathe in the blood of your enemies, you will probably like this book.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464216650i/19213612.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>Shelly would like it!</i><br/><br/>So, not the most original of ideas: two types of vampire - good & evil. The good ones have to find a mate and get her preggo within 30 days. They then have a set of twins - one good, one evil. The evil twin is sacrificed and the good one is kept. Sounds reasonable, </span>
  <span id="freeText13869613078988126516" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464216650i/19213611.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Rape, Torture, Murder, Dismemberment, Bloody Battles, and Explicit Sex... This book has it all!<br><br>If you like Paranormal Romance, but also want to bathe in the blood of your enemies, you will probably like this book.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464216650i/19213612.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Shelly would like it!</i><br><br>So, not the most original of ideas: two types of vampire - good &amp; evil. The good ones have to find a mate and get her preggo within 30 days. They then have a set of twins - one good, one evil. The evil twin is sacrificed and the good one is kept. Sounds reasonable, huh?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464216650i/19213613.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Our couple today is Jocelyn and Nathaniel. She's a human FBI agent investigating human trafficking and he is a thousand year old vampire. They must have tons in common, right?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464216650i/19213614.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>cute couple!</i><br><br>Here's the thing, though... The synopsis talks about her investigating human trafficking, and she mentions it...in passing, but if you are expecting a mystery or cool FBI sting you are in for a disappointment. The whole human trafficking thing lasts for a couple of sentences. Most of the time is spent with Nathaniel being a pushy alpha, Jocelyn angsting over her circumstances, and lots and lots of bloody killing. I liked the bloody killing best! :)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1464216650ra/19213615.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> sooo delicious...</i><br><br></span>

<div id="review_1470094095" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1470094095" />
    <a title="Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed"><img alt="Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1455042547p2/22911953.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1470094095?book_show_action=true">Dec 15, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠" href="/user/show/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed">Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed?shelf=2016">2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1470094095" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7949977835840461179">I think I read this book wrong. Several of my friends posted warnings in their reviews that this book and series were super super bloody and violent. This confused me, I didn't find it excessively gory. It's probably because I'm inured to such from reading and watching murder mysteries + I'm an evil axe wielding murderous penguin. <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392169502i/8512058.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>How I felt after reading this book and wondering where the massive amounts of blood everyone said were. (P.S. I feel odd posting a pic of your beloved, Future Jess, bu</i></span>
  <span id="freeText7949977835840461179" style="display:none">I think I read this book wrong. Several of my friends posted warnings in their reviews that this book and series were super super bloody and violent. This confused me, I didn't find it excessively gory. It's probably because I'm inured to such from reading and watching murder mysteries + I'm an evil axe wielding murderous penguin. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392169502i/8512058.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>How I felt after reading this book and wondering where the massive amounts of blood everyone said were. (P.S. I feel odd posting a pic of your beloved, Future Jess, but his confused face fit this perfectly)</i><br><br>The plot of the book is fine - vampire guy must mate with his destined mate before 30 days are up, avenge his brother's death by the bad vampire guys, and avoid the bad guys killing his destiny lady. See, it's fine, the problem is the romance.....::::crickets::::....there is no romance! Do not tell me that shit storm that went on between the female mc, Jocelyn, &amp; male mc, Nathaniel, is romance, because it's not, unless you're using roofies and mind control on the chick. It's worthless. She's out following human trafficking leads, stumbles upon a bad vamp being bad, meets up with Nate (someone needs to give him a nickname and it's obviously me because I'm not typing out his long ass name each time, it's annoying), there's attraction, but she's got police shit to do and says bye. Not so fast little lady, the moon has to go wonky and proclaim her Nate's destiny (how they refer to their mates) and he has to seal the deal with her within 30 days or die horribly. She's not too keen on vampires after seeing the bad vamp kill a woman, so she runs screaming, and keeps trying to escape Nate. He catches her, obviously, and somehow, SOMEHOW, somehow, she starts feeling tingly for him and wanting to jump his bones, and somehow she's now in love with him. There's no progression of their romance, it's just 'hey, we're in love now, we've barely talked, my brother constantly threatens you, and you hate vamps, but somehow we've fallen in love without any sort of progression and I'm totally cool with you knocking me up with twins and sacrificing one of them.'<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462992735ra/19070331.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The whole knocking the destiny girl up with twins and then sacrificing the 'evil' one is bollocks. How do they know if the kid will grow up to be a serial killer like the bad vamps. There are plenty of bad people in the world that don't do anything murderous. Also, I really don't like anything with child killing in it. If I wanted to read about dead babies, I'd read <i>Angela's Ashes.</i> I'm not too pleased with Jocelyn only putting up a tiny protest about Nate sacrificing the dark twin. If that was me, I would've pulled a silver machete on him and threatened his man bits. Where's the whole love your spawn maternal instinct thing? <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469794646i/19858657.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>In case you couldn't tell, I'm not too keen on the main couple. Jocelyn is TSTL and Nate is an asshole. The secondary characters are Nate's brothers - Marquis Silivasi (his name reminds me of the Marquis de Sade), and whatever the other ones are named. The youngest brother is sweet and kind and his little charge is a nice distraction. Marquis on the other hand, he's a straight up bitchy bastard. He is domineering and mean to his brothers, he outright threatens Jocelyn from the instant he sees her, and he's cruel to inept children. I don't care if he's lonely and sad, stop being a douche and maybe someone would love you. He annoyed me. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469788491i/19857244.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Doubtful this will surprise anyone, but I preferred the bad vampire guys to the good ones. There are several parts that are from their POV's. Just about every character got their own POV stint. The bad guys are advertised as bad, they're literally born bad, their bicolor hair proclaims they're bad, and they like being bad. I'm cool with them, because they're not telling me they're good and then being douchey like Nate and his clan.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469794646ra/19858658.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> Just a warning, there is a detailed rape scene. I skimmed it, like I did the majority of this book, but it doesn't end in death. The bad vamps do kill every chance they get, and they spawn like the creature from Alien.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469788694i/19857355._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>As to the violence and blood in this....well of course there's lots of blood, it's a vampire book. There are multiple fights, so more blood going on there. But it's not like there was a set of elevators filled with blood that coursed through the halls like in The Shining, and with that are your standard, it falls short. All in all, I was bored with this book and skimmed it mainly because I was so bored, but some reason I pushed myself to finish it. I kept thinking it had to get better somewhere, or more interesting; it didn't. I may try another in the series since several of my friends rate the books well, but it's not a priority. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469788491ra/19857246.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="7949977835840461179" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10559653604176043008"><br/><i>Blood Destiny</i> is the first book in Tessa Dawn's <i>Blood Curse</i> series and the start to an exciting series. <br/><br/>I have to say, I was pretty excited to find out about this series because I adore vampires but they've been done to death and I'm pretty sure I've read them all. <i>Blood Destiny</i> is edgy, fast paced and sexy, with vampires, shifters, mages, gods and goddess making up this unique world and complex characters. The writing isn't perfect in that there were some moments of cheesiness and the telepathi</span>
  <span id="freeText10559653604176043008" style="display:none"><br /><i>Blood Destiny</i> is the first book in Tessa Dawn's <i>Blood Curse</i> series and the start to an exciting series. <br /><br />I have to say, I was pretty excited to find out about this series because I adore vampires but they've been done to death and I'm pretty sure I've read them all. <i>Blood Destiny</i> is edgy, fast paced and sexy, with vampires, shifters, mages, gods and goddess making up this unique world and complex characters. The writing isn't perfect in that there were some moments of cheesiness and the telepathic communications were not italicized, so it wasn't always clear whether we were actually hearing dialog exchanges or thought processing. So yeah, not perfect, but not bad, either.<br /><br />I'm looking forward to reading more of the series!<br /><br />3.5/5 stars<br /></span>

<div id="review_1006769963" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1006769963" />
    <a title="Marta Cox" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14378267-marta-cox"><img alt="Marta Cox" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605691858p2/14378267.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1006769963?book_show_action=true">Jul 25, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marta Cox" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marta Cox" href="/user/show/14378267-marta-cox">Marta Cox</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14378267-marta-cox?shelf=my-reviews">my-reviews</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1006769963" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12735411591342648399">I've had this series recommended to me with such passion by close friends that I had to give it a try. I confess the pricing initially put me off but I noticed that recently it's not as exorbitant so was really happy to finally give it a go. I will admit that the Blood Curse series has quite an unusual way of setting up with two very different types of cursed vampires but I'm sorry for me the first twenty five percent or so was very similar to a series I've read featuring dark vampires from the </span>
  <span id="freeText12735411591342648399" style="display:none">I've had this series recommended to me with such passion by close friends that I had to give it a try. I confess the pricing initially put me off but I noticed that recently it's not as exorbitant so was really happy to finally give it a go. I will admit that the Blood Curse series has quite an unusual way of setting up with two very different types of cursed vampires but I'm sorry for me the first twenty five percent or so was very similar to a series I've read featuring dark vampires from the Carpathian mountains . Not exactly the same granted but there are quite a few similarities in their manner and abilities but truth be told we are all influenced by something I guess. I kept on reading ( hey I trust my friends recommendations ) and once past thirty percent got far more involved in the story and how it would all play out.<br />I'm not sure I really liked Nathaniel as he didn't really give Jocelyn much choice and yes I know they meet at what is a very emotional time for him but I really wanted and expected a little more finesse. Jocelyn is supposed to be this hard nosed agent trying to uncover human trafficking but what she finds herself embroiled in is something far more dangerous. I understand that the supernatural world was a shock and scary but hmm I just didn't believe how she initially reacted. <br />Now I do have to say that the idea of the blood curse these guys are under is very interesting and there does seem quite a lot of scope to expand this world. The 'good' vampires are still quite scary and the 'bad' even more so but what is expected of Jocelyn and Nathaniel turned my stomach. This book may feature a close knit family but the author does not sugar coat things and it's both violent and harrowing at times . I will also confess the author had me completely changing my opinion of one of the brothers who I initially wanted to drop kick! So yes it wasn't a perfect read for me but sufficiently different to make me keen to read more. Oh and even though the couple are 'fated' the romance wasn't thrust down the readers throat and when the couple finally came together it seemed appropriate. </span>
  <a data-text-id="12735411591342648399" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Had me COMPLETELY grossed out &amp; confused. Yet, I still could not look away. I didn't even realize I was sucked in til the "sucking" was almost over.<br><br>This book is <b>AMAZING!</b> I mean I'm like...<br><a href="http://s1135.photobucket.com/user/Enhya77/media/7289235_zpsa59cb7a8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388435609ra/7834599.gif" alt=" photo 7289235_zpsa59cb7a8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There is so much going on here. There is ALOT of set up. But everything that occurs is interesting. There is brutality here, so please be warned. But it's not for brutality's sake. It all feels organic and just flows within the story.<br><br>The set up, premise &amp; plot, the why's of it all, is just done superbly.<br>The romance with the main characters <b>Nathaniel &amp; Jocelyn</b> I really loved. I love the dynamic with these two. And I just love <b>Nathaniel</b> period. *pants* They just jump off of the page for me. I felt what they were going through. I felt all of the characters in this way, to be honest. Even the Villains. And let me just say..<br><a href="http://s1135.photobucket.com/user/Enhya77/media/4986510_zps088d24fd.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385144031ra/7079392.gif" alt=" photo 4986510_zps088d24fd.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>is wrong with them? They will have you off your rocker with some of the stuff that goes on here. Even our "Heroes" will do this to you in some instances.<br><br>It was all just a cluster of <i>"I can't believe this sh*t"</i> greatness. And I can't believe I had not read this series yet.<br><br><b>Be Warned</b> this is dark. It's Brutal. It's Intense. But it's also Beautiful, Heart warming, Heartbreaking, Lustful, Erotic &amp; Loving.<br>I am running off to start book 2 now. I think I may have found another Vamp series worthy of my attention. I only hope each journey within this series gets better &amp; better for me.<br><br>I would HIGHLY recommend this read. PLEASE read in order. There was alot of character set up here that feels like it serves for a huge foundation for future books. This does end with an HEA <br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="15694341040086216356" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_249690463" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/249690463" />
    <a title=" ~V~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3284461-v"><img alt=" ~V~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1426478543p2/3284461.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/249690463?book_show_action=true">Dec 21, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" ~V~" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" ~V~" href="/user/show/3284461-v"> ~V~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3284461-v?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer249690463" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer790115823497773744">** 3 1/2 stars **<br/><br/>This was a pretty good first book in the Blood Curse series. I read this with my friend, Sharon, and i agree with her that there are some similarities with Christine Feehan's Carpathian series...and it's mostly because of the way these vampires carry themselves/act and speak to their woman...very old school vampire novel. <br/><br/>I would have to say that the one thing i didn't care for much was the romance between the two main characters..well...at least in the 1st half of the book...ac</span>
  <span id="freeText790115823497773744" style="display:none">** 3 1/2 stars **<br /><br />This was a pretty good first book in the Blood Curse series. I read this with my friend, Sharon, and i agree with her that there are some similarities with Christine Feehan's Carpathian series...and it's mostly because of the way these vampires carry themselves/act and speak to their woman...very old school vampire novel. <br /><br />I would have to say that the one thing i didn't care for much was the romance between the two main characters..well...at least in the 1st half of the book...actually...there was NO romance between those two in the 1st half of the book! It was them meeting and him basically taking her and telling her that she was HIS and that was it...she'll "learn" to love him...THAT is very Carpathian! LOL! I realize a lot of books in this genre are quick in the romance department but i do like a little bit more finesse from the "guy" when he finds his mate. Not that Nathaniel wasn't sweet with her..there was just not a whole lot of "getting to know each other" AT ALL...no build up whatsoever. It's also not often that a heroine annoys me..it takes quite a bit actually...but for some reason i did not care for Jocelyn for the entire first half of this book either...she was VERY "woe is me" and wimpy...which i find kind of odd being as how she's a cop...i think she definitely should have acted stronger because of that!<br /><br />Having said all of that..i DID actually enjoy this book. I really loved the whole "blood curse" (light and dark descendents of Jadon and Jagaer, and how you could tell them apart by the color of their hair..sons of Jadon.."the good/light ones" had black hair w/ bands of blue and the sons of Jagaer..."the evil/dark ones" had black hair w/ bands of red)..i thought that was very unique and very interesting! I loved that they had WINGS...a 6ft span of FEATHERED WINGS! THAT was cool! Another thing i found rather refreshing was the violence. Not that i'm a lover of violence (SBY ;) teehee)... but this author does NOT sugar coat ANYTHING! Nothing is insinuated...it's all out there for you to "see"...some people who don't care to read about such graphic violence ie:<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[someone having their heart ripped out through the throat <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> may be turned off by this but for some reason, it just didn't bother me...even though they were "good" ...it kinda fit with the type of vampires/warriors they were.<br /><br />Ok..i'll wrap this up but i wanted to mention one more thing... i really loved all of Nathaniel's brothers..how close and protective they were of each other. Although i didn't care for the oldest brother, Marquis, at first..he was rather barbaric and kind of a jerk. But i ended up REALLY liking him a lot by the end! I loved the whole scene with him and Joelle...he was sooo sweet with her and it was heartbreaking! :( The epilogue has definitely set things up for his book which is next and i can't wait to read it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="790115823497773744" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5138258368017853994">I really don't know how to go about this book. You see, I know I have a tons of friends that if they read this all hell would break loose. Yet by the end I still have a slight inclination to read the next one, albeit, a small one. <br/><br/>It's just that the list of cons could go on and on... and on. For starters, Nathaniel is an abusive boyfriend. No, he doesn't hit her but what do you think when she knows she angered him when she disagreed about anything and when he comes for her she basically runs the</span>
  <span id="freeText5138258368017853994" style="display:none">I really don't know how to go about this book. You see, I know I have a tons of friends that if they read this all hell would break loose. Yet by the end I still have a slight inclination to read the next one, albeit, a small one. <br /><br />It's just that the list of cons could go on and on... and on. For starters, Nathaniel is an abusive boyfriend. No, he doesn't hit her but what do you think when she knows she angered him when she disagreed about anything and when he comes for her she basically runs the other way because she's afraid of how he'll respond. <br /><br />His jealously reached psychotic levels to the point of taking her voice away because she talked to another male. <br /><br />His touching her felt rapey, because she would constantly move away and he'd keep trying to put his hands on her. <br /><br />She was only safe when she agreed with him. Any other time they argued she was reprimanded like a child with no thought process. <br /><br />Dear Lord, and that was just that mayor peeves that irked me about the male lead. Then we have the plot, the secondary characters, the dialogue, and the female lead. Just hoping you get my drift. <br /><br />P.s. Excuse any and all Grammer errors and the sloppy layout, it was from my phone </span>

<div id="review_315654767" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/315654767" />
    <a title="Vallsykes" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5164414-vallsykes"><img alt="Vallsykes" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1367067514p2/5164414.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/315654767?book_show_action=true">Apr 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vallsykes" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vallsykes" href="/user/show/5164414-vallsykes">Vallsykes</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/10067360-blood-destiny">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=villain-gets-his-15min">villain-gets-his-15min</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=violence">violence</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=wtf-conflict">wtf-conflict</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=need-refresher">need-refresher</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=wolf-and-lamb">wolf-and-lamb</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=more-than-3-stars">more-than-3-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=were-wolves-and-shifters">were-wolves-and-shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=secondary-character-steals-the-show">secondary-character-steals-the-show</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=great-storyline">great-storyline</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5164414-vallsykes?shelf=vampires-and-fangs">vampires-and-fangs</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer315654767" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9752437453771395413"><b>3.5 stars</b><br/>The mythos: the Blood Curse which is put on the vamps, who are human descendants of an ancient royal family. One concession of this curse is that some of these descendants get to have a destined mate, and has to convert-her-or-die. Yet, while reading this cumbersome tale of these descendants, divided by two brothers, two houses, good and evil, and twins begetting twins, I couldn't help but hope for cleverer dialogue and connection to character( the couple).<br/> <br/>From the ancient royals, twin</span>
  <span id="freeText9752437453771395413" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars</b><br />The mythos: the Blood Curse which is put on the vamps, who are human descendants of an ancient royal family. One concession of this curse is that some of these descendants get to have a destined mate, and has to convert-her-or-die. Yet, while reading this cumbersome tale of these descendants, divided by two brothers, two houses, good and evil, and twins begetting twins, I couldn't help but hope for cleverer dialogue and connection to character( the couple).<br /> <br />From the ancient royals, twin brothers, Jaeger and Jadon, are like Cain and Abel, one evil, one good. Despite this, both are cursed that they and all there descendants have to give up their first born son as a sacrifice for all the lives taken by the evil brother and not protected by the good brother(history of this is vague). Therein, we meet the hero, who is a descendant of Jadon, the good one. We meet his brothers and of course, a few descendants of the bad twin.<br /><br />From there come the painful births suffered by human women who carry the evil ones' seed, the painful conversions of the human female mates allowed only to the descendants of Jadon, and the skirmishes between the good ones and their evil cousin counterparts. Last but not least, comes central characters, the human female mate who meets her vampire destiny and fights against the idea that there are actually Vampires...until its too late or until she miraculously accepts the inevitable. Not too clever.<br /><br />This book did not wow me with the erotic encounters <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[(H and h only have actual sex two times after 80% of book. During(and immediately after) that one-two bam sequence, the heroine is converted to vamp and has a baby within 48hrs (LOL, this is not the only thing in this plot that can be construed as a "raw deal for the woman") <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Moreover, the chemistry between the hero and his lady was ...meh. In fact, I forget when his lady said she loved him back, and though he said it first, during sex, and he showed <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[some tears during her conversion <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, I just didn't feel the love.<br /><br />However, I felt the power. Tessa Dawn spent more time writing inside the Vamps' heads(the good and the bad­). The grief for loved one is depicted with emotion, and details of strategies against enemies racked up so much that it was more like reading a combat video game than a PNR. But, I liked the action and the powers each vamp possessed. <br /><br />The author took this epic-ness further by adding more enemies: werewolves. This made it necessary for good and bad vamps to unite in some instances (thus the delicious evil vamp Saber is introduced). And if werewolves didn't produce enough gray area in this good vs. evil saga, then the epilogue spills the beans on <i>another</i> ancient one. Due to the blood curse, she is an anomaly.<br /><br />Honestly, all of that makes the reader want to continue the series, but it makes one wary also(Will the story get better?). The author could sell short on the romance or the clarity of <i>how to break the curse</i> (I mean this is the main purpose for reading it, right? The conflict <i>and</i> the romance). <br /><br />Giving more advantage/power to the female characters would be a good thing too.<br /><br />I hope the next book is as involved and is better.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9752437453771395413" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/138671189?book_show_action=true">Jan 05, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Megan Riverina Romantics" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Megan Riverina Romantics" href="/user/show/4453888-megan-riverina-romantics">Megan Riverina Romantics</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4453888-megan-riverina-romantics?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4453888-megan-riverina-romantics?shelf=audiobook-audible">audiobook-audible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4453888-megan-riverina-romantics?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4453888-megan-riverina-romantics?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4453888-megan-riverina-romantics?shelf=dark-fantasy">dark-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4453888-megan-riverina-romantics?shelf=nookbook">nookbook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4453888-megan-riverina-romantics?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer138671189" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4944675468347367902">I won this book from <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.goodreads.com/'>http://www.goodreads.com/</a><br/><br/> Tessa Dawn introduces us to a new type of vampire in her new book Blood Destiny. Blood Destiny is book 1 in the Blood Curse Series.<br/><br/> Nathaniel Silivasi is a descendant of the Celestial Being Jadon. He is a vampire, a being of both darkness and light. His job as an Ancient Master Warrior vampire is to protect the Earth and it's inhabitants from the Dark Ones. His truly evil vampire brethren, the descendants of Jeager.<br/><br/> Jocelyn Levi works for ICE, a hig</span>
  <span id="freeText4944675468347367902" style="display:none">I won this book from <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/">http://www.goodreads.com/</a><br /><br /> Tessa Dawn introduces us to a new type of vampire in her new book Blood Destiny. Blood Destiny is book 1 in the Blood Curse Series.<br /><br /> Nathaniel Silivasi is a descendant of the Celestial Being Jadon. He is a vampire, a being of both darkness and light. His job as an Ancient Master Warrior vampire is to protect the Earth and it's inhabitants from the Dark Ones. His truly evil vampire brethren, the descendants of Jeager.<br /><br /> Jocelyn Levi works for ICE, a highly specialized department of Homeland Security. She's been investigating a human-trafficking ring for months. This particular ring was different from the norm though. It seemed as if the victims were being taken for sacrifices in ritualistic killings. She just couldn't figure out by whom though. She hoped that the newest lead that she was following would yield some answers. What she got, as she entered the caves located in the Eastern Rocky Mountains, was a whole lot more.<br /><br /> I so totally love the world that Tessa Dawn has created in her Blood Curse Series. She has created a brand new type of vampire to entertain us. It was really great to see where her vampires came from and their religious belief system. The prologue did a wonderful job of introducing us to this new world and the hierarchy that the descendants of Jadon follow is given to us in an easy to follow format later on in the book.<br /><br /> In 800 BC, the Celestial Beings had all but become extinct because the men became too mad in their endless blood lust. Finally the royal Romanian Demir twins, Jeager and Jadon, were brought before their accusers, The Blood of countless female victims, for their punishment and revenge. Because their many crimes were against women they were cursed to never feel the love or companionship of a female or have female children. They would always have sons in sets of two, spawned of humans who would die terrible deaths upon giving birth, and both sons would be evil. Also the firstborn son of the first set of twins would need to be sacrificed. If this sacrifice of atonement was not made the penalty would be a horrible death. To make sure that they truly suffered, they would be made immortal, forced to drink the blood of innocents and remain in the darkness of night. This curse would follow them and their descendants for all time. Jadon begged mercy from his accusers. Though he was with the warriors when they performed their heinous acts, he didn't kill anybody. And while he never stopped them to save an innocent he tried to go after the guilty parties. He was not truly evil at heart and he begged that they have mercy on him and his house. After searching his soul the accusers amended his curse. He and his descendants would be able to walk in the daylight and while they would have to subsist on blood they needn't kill to do so. Though they still couldn't have female children, they would have one chance at finding a mate and there would be signs as to who that may be. Finally, The sacrifice of a child would still have to be made but one of the firstborn twins will be a dark one, and he would be the sacrifice. Saving the lighter, purer one, to carry on his line.<br /><br /> When Jocelyn meets Nathaniel she is absolutely terrified from what she's witnessed in the cave. He's just come from burying his youngest brother. His COD? His inability to adhere to the Blood Curse. Not the best time for the signs of his own mate entering his life to show up. So even though he originally tells Jocelyn that he'll allow her to go home he knows he must not. The ensuing trials of their relationship are evenly matched with the battles that Nathaniel and his brothers fight with the Dark Ones. And I must say...battle they do! I have one word for you...eunuch! <br /><br /> Even though this book is marketed as a dark fantasy I feel that paranormal romance readers will enjoy it as well. As well as urban fantasy readers. I truly feel that this is one of those books that ventures into all these categories. It's a fabulous start to what is looking like a fantastic series. I can't wait for book 2, Blood Awakening to come out!<br /><br /> On a slightly different note...I found this book on the side bar of my facebook page. I looked it up and quickly decided that I wanted to read it. So of course I friend requested Tessa. Then I started to follow her on goodreads where we are also friends. I entered a "first-read" contest on goodreads to win a copy of the book but I couldn't wait so I ended up ordering it. Then guess what? I ended up winning it from goodreads the day after I ordered it! Great luck right? But that's not all that I've been lucky in in regards to this book. I've given you this brief synapses of my relationship with Tessa Dawn because I feel that it really needs to be known that she cares about her fans. It is a rare thing indeed to find an author who will take a second and jot a note off about whatever to her fans. And Tessa is one of those authors.<br /><br />AUDIOBOOK reread - 11/2015</span>
  <a data-text-id="4944675468347367902" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6566046610324232519">Let me start with: this was a mistake. In all senses. I bought it thinking I was sampling it, and I kept reading. So... mistake upon mistake. My bad.<br/><br/>That said, this book was revolting in a very personal way. <br/><br/>I don't find anything good, nor romantic in the idea that I was created for someone. There's all that pesky free will that is ignored or directly strangled in this kind of books. Is that supposed to make me feel special? Nope, no way. Ok, that's on me.<br/>But it's definitely on the author when s</span>
  <span id="freeText6566046610324232519" style="display:none">Let me start with: this was a mistake. In all senses. I bought it thinking I was sampling it, and I kept reading. So... mistake upon mistake. My bad.<br /><br />That said, this book was revolting in a very personal way. <br /><br />I don't find anything good, nor romantic in the idea that I was created for someone. There's all that pesky free will that is ignored or directly strangled in this kind of books. Is that supposed to make me feel special? Nope, no way. Ok, that's on me.<br />But it's definitely on the author when she doesn't realize that in 72 hours there's no love, and so you have to be particularly skilled to make me feel anything but contempt for the characters. (In her defense, I haven't found such an author....) <br /><br />What you are giving me is a slave (she has no choice, and that's hammered on, even with the threat of violence) that's forced to change her frigging race to save from death a guy she has literally just met and give him 2 sons to boot. Oh by the way, one has to be killed on birth so his father can live.... So, let's not be started on how revolting is the idea that one is evil because he is of one peculiar race.... Nope. no way...<br /><br />Then there's the story in itself, again I blame the author. Why writing such a blurb when it's all a lie? Why telling us the heroine is a frigging homeland security detective, and a good one too, when it's all a lie. The heroine's past is hinted but had no role here. Moreover, she's stupid, weak, TSL and in no way coherent with such past. And the one time she thinks for herself, she's punished severely by the author who goes to extreme to make it happen. She's betrayed by a friend who tries to rape her. The extreme isn't the rape, it's the fact the author does what she wants with her world with no respect for readers. The friend is supposed to know who she is before any revelation (three years before the actual revelation) and uses her as a bait. Uh?? <br /><br />Why would I want to side with a violent race with no respect for humans (they have no problems in raping their minds and going on a killing spree) and even less for women?<br /><br />I could go on, but others have done a very good job already:<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1869042826">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a> <br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1755471281">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a> <br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/155647024">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1415067587934878323"><u>Incredibly good book!</u> Not for the faint of heart... there is a lot of graphic violence. There is some smex, but this isn't standard erotica where there is a 15 page smex scene every 10.5 pages... there are actually about 3 of them and two are good/loving, one is sort of violent. Not your JR Ward vamps for sure! The Silivasi vamps are truly butt-kickers! But, I loved them all and will be pre-ordering the next book.<br/><br/>I am impressed with Tessa Dawn's writing and her ability to make the characters lov</span>
  <span id="freeText1415067587934878323" style="display:none"><u>Incredibly good book!</u> Not for the faint of heart... there is a lot of graphic violence. There is some smex, but this isn't standard erotica where there is a 15 page smex scene every 10.5 pages... there are actually about 3 of them and two are good/loving, one is sort of violent. Not your JR Ward vamps for sure! The Silivasi vamps are truly butt-kickers! But, I loved them all and will be pre-ordering the next book.<br /><br />I am impressed with Tessa Dawn's writing and her ability to make the characters loving as well as showing their extremely violent sides... they are complicated. There is much heartbreak and violence in their lives and yet they are able to very tender.<br /><br />The 'Epilogue' was just as awesome as the previous story... sets you up in extreme anticipation for the next book.<br /><br />The book had very few spelling or editing errors, also a pleasure.<br /><br />I will certainly be reading this again before the release of book 2 in October 2011.<br /><br /></span>

    <a title="Diana (Offbeat Vagabond)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4571498-diana-offbeat-vagabond"><img alt="Diana (Offbeat Vagabond)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1362102807p2/4571498.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Diana (Offbeat Vagabond)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Diana (Offbeat Vagabond)" href="/user/show/4571498-diana-offbeat-vagabond">Diana (Offbeat Vagabond)</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer151190084" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12960925326804824993">Finished this last night. Easily one of the best books I have ever read. Yes, I said it and I mean it. Review coming tomorrow. YAY!<br/><br/>Review poster here: <a href='http://offbeatvagabond.blogspot.com/2011/05/review-blood-destiny-blood-curse-1-by.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>http://offbeatvagabond.blogspot.com/2011/05/review-blood-destiny-blood-curse-1-by.html</a><br/><br/><br/> HOLY SHIT! That is all I can say about this book. I am going to say something only because it is absolutely true; this is one of the BEST books I have read in my life. It is everything I ever wanted my vampires to be, scary as hell and yet too sexy for your eyes</span>
  <span id="freeText12960925326804824993" style="display:none">Finished this last night. Easily one of the best books I have ever read. Yes, I said it and I mean it. Review coming tomorrow. YAY!<br /><br />Review poster here: <a href="http://offbeatvagabond.blogspot.com/2011/05/review-blood-destiny-blood-curse-1-by.html" rel="nofollow noopener">http://offbeatvagabond.blogspot.com/2011/05/review-blood-destiny-blood-curse-1-by.html</a><br /><br /><br /> HOLY SHIT! That is all I can say about this book. I am going to say something only because it is absolutely true; this is one of the BEST books I have read in my life. It is everything I ever wanted my vampires to be, scary as hell and yet too sexy for your eyes. Now with the exception of a few vampires (Dante, Bones, all of the BDB, etc.), there aren't many vampires that are truly brutal, I mean X-Rated, B-Movie brutal. Well I don't have to look any further, I found them right here in Blood Destiny. Tessa Dawn, you are now in my top five list of kickass authors. Thank you!<br /><br /><br /> Blood Destiny starts with telling us about the existence of vampires. There are two different kinds of vampires, light and dark. Twin brothers, Jadon (light) and Jaegar (dark) were punished by the blood of the women they killed. But Jadon wasn't the one who spilled blood, it was the vicious Jaegar. But nonetheless, they were both cursed. The light vampires can walk in the sun and have mates. Their mates have been chosen by the gods. Thing is they only have thirty days to marry and have twins with their mate (the vamps only have twin boys) and sacrifice the evil twin. If they don't, their lives will be at risk. The dark vampires do not get a mate which complicates things because when they do, things end badly for the women they take.<br /><br /><br /> Oh my goodness, I loved this book sooooo much. I didn't know what to think of this book when I first heard about it. My favorite thing about it was Tessa Dawn's take on vampire mythology. Honestly, throw out everything you know about vampires because it will not apply to this book. The vampires are scary, truly immortal (only way to kill them is through draining them completely of blood), and they aren't only powerful, they are part gods. Seriously, the things they can do are insane. They can literally control the elements with their emotions. For instance, when Nathaniel found out what happened to his recently deceased brother's, Shelby, wife Dalia, he got so pissed, he caused an earthquake. Even more so, they have abilities they gain that literally takes over a thousand years of education to master. Seriously, do not screw with these guys.<br /><br /><br /> The characters were incredible. The protege Braden and the Silivasi brothers were a riot especially Marquis, who was the meanest of them all. But he had a heart of gold. Well you don't see that until near the end of the book. Marquis does everything to protect his brothers and being the oldest of them all, he carries a huge weight on his shoulders. I also loved the leading lady, Jocelyn. She had a pair of lady balls for sure. After everything she has seen (and what she tried to do to escape), she fights no matter what. I loved that it wasn't one of those things where she immediately decided to be with Nathaniel. She actually thought about what she was getting into. I loved Nathaniel. He was hot and brutal when he needed to be and loved Jocelyn unconditionally.<br /><br /><br /> Now for the warning. This book will not be for everyone. Do not let the fact that this is part Paranormal Romance fool you. There are some horrific scenes in this book. I mean scenes they wouldn't put in a horror movie. Blood Destiny is very dark, cruel and doesn't hold anything back. If you are looking for sweet little vampires that glitter and sparkle, look elsewhere. If you want vampires that actually belong in a horror movie and will literally rip you to shreds, these are your guys. <br /><br /><br /> I can't think of anything bad to say about this book. The story and history in this book was rich and well-layered. Again, the mythology is super fresh and unique. Do not go into this thinking it is just another vampire book, it is far from it. This is an amazing debut by Tessa Dawn and this is high, very high on my favorites list. Marquis' book is book 2, Blood Awakening, and it comes out October 28th. So I plan on reading this one or two more times before then. And many more times after that and I am sure Blood Awakening will be just as re-readable.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12960925326804824993" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
